Let's make a game!
  name:Wall Destroyer
  by:Tellurium
  created:04/21/2014
  updated:11/10/2024
  version:3.1

Settings
  building cost increase:110%
  building cost refund:75%
  stylesheet:https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Qjuh/walldestroyer/refs/heads/main/stylesheet.txt

Layout
  *main
    contains:buildings, clickables, resources, upgrades
  
  *clickables
    contains:tag:clickable, tag:textbutton
    names:hide

  *resources
    contains:Resources
    header:Resources
    no tooltip
  
  *buildings
    contains:BulkDisplay, tag:wall, tag:building
  
  *upgrades
    contains:Upgrades
    header:Upgrades

  *log
    contains:Log

Buttons
  *hitWall
  on click:
    gain 1 money
    gain 1 totalMoney
    gain 1 handDamage
  end
  shown
  name:Punch wall
  class:hitwall
  tag:clickable
  icon:http://i.imgur.com/108BtPH.png
  desc:Made <b>[handDamage] damage</b> by hand

Buildings

  *timeCounter
  on tick:
    if (resetTimes >= 1) gain 0.016666666666666666666666666666 timeSinceReset
    gain 0.016666666666666666666666666666 timePlayed
  end
  always hidden
  start with:1

  *makeBricks
  on earn:
    gain 1 handBricks
    gain 1 bricks
    gain 1 totalBricks
  end
  name:Create Bricks
  tags:clickable loseonreset
  class:makebricks
  icon:http://i.imgur.com/Tdh80P1.png
  req:have handBrickUnlock
  desc:Created <b>[handBricks] bricks</b> by hand

  *reset
  on click:
    gain prePrestige prestige
    gain goldBricks timesWon
    gain bonusBossBrick bonusBossPoint
    gain spaceBossBrick spaceBossPoint
    gain timeBossBrick timeBossPoint
    gain endBossBrick endBossPoint
    gain winBricks timesActuallyWon
    gain 1 resetTimes
    lose resetUnlock
    lose finalWallUnlock
    hide lastBuilding
    gain wallsDestroyed totalWalls
    lose tag:loseonreset
    show destroyWall
    toast Time Rewound: Your cosmic knowledge has been converted into future knowledge capsules.
    toast The Time Bear is coming.
  end
  name:Rewind time (Removes all buildings & resources, converts cosmic knowledge into prestige)
  class:textbutton
  req:have resetUnlock
  no buy
  
  *damageConverter
  on click:
    gain (totalMoney * 0.0000000000000000000000000000000005) prePrestige
    lose totalMoney
  end
  name:Convert all damage to cosmic knowledge
  class:textbutton
  req:have damageConvUnlock
  no buy

  *destroyWall
  desc:Destroy the wall and move on to a bigger one.</>Gives <b>25</b> bricks.</>Awards <b>250,000,000,000</b> cash.</>Worth <b>1</b> cosmic knowledge.
  cost:1000000000000 totalMoney
  on earn:
    gain 250000000000 money
    gain 25 bricks
    gain 25 totalBricks
    gain 1 wallsDestroyed
    gain 1 prePrestige
    hide this
  end
  name:Destroy wall
  tags:loseonreset wall
  class:plainwall wall
  shown
  *destroyBigWall

  on earn:
    gain 25000000000000 money
